90a5(mdo sde): tu na sems can la ra mda' bya zhing bsgral ba'i chos thub du zos pa la mang du shes pa dang / nyung ngu mthong ba la/ mang du rig pa dang / yi ge'i ri me mang du ma btsal bar gdu
90a6(mdo sde): gi mngon rtags thob pa yang bshad kyis/ byed la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' rnams kun sems gcig tu brtag pa ra nyon gcig dang / khyed la dgrol bshad do// sems can
90a7(mdo sde): thams cad kun sems gcig sangs rgyas gcig/ ngo bo nyid gcig ste/ mya ngan 'brug pa thams cad kun ni sems gcig las skyeso// kun kyang 'du mched dang / shes rab gnyis kyi
90a8(mdo sde): gnas kyi rgya las langs// tsi lha zhes byas na rgyu'i rang bzhin dang / bdag gi rang bzhin dang / rang bzhin gnyis kyi stobs las/ sdengs rnam gnyis kyi rang bzhin g.yos te/ sra
90b1(mdo sde): cig bsams pa las mi bden pa'i sems skyes te/ mi bden pa de la ni phyi mo 'ang med do// skad cig sems g.yos pa'i tshe/ mya ngan 'khrug pa'ang mod bzhin ldang ngo // sems 'di la brtags
90b2(mdo sde): ni mi bden pa'i sems la phyi mo med de phyi mo med na gnas kyang med do// de la gnas med par rtogs na tshor ba'i sems skyes te/ phyi mo tsher ba'i sems gtsang ma la bsam pa yong med
90b3(mdo sde): do// sems la bsam pa med na sems mi g.yo'o// sems mi g.yo na sems kyi gnas med de/ de'i ming ni gtsang gdang ngo // gtsang gdang ba'i stong pa'i sems ni ngo bo nyid phyi ma

90b5(mdo sde): ni gtsang gdang ba'i sems la bya ba yang med/ g.yo ba ya nga med dri ma yang med gtsang ma yang med/ skye ba yang med/ 'bri 'i yang med de/ mthar cis kyang gos pa med de/ gnas gci
90b6(mdo sde): la'ang 'dug pa med de/ de'i ming dang grangs las yong bral lo// rtag pa de bzhin na de bzhin zhes pa yang med de/ dper na rdo rje'i dang mtshungs te ngo bo nyid gcig pu la zhig pa'ang med
90b7(mdo sde): // deper na na mkha' dang mtshungs te thams cad shong / dper me tog pad+mo dang mtshungs te sred pa'i chus mi chag so// las 'di spyad na yang dag par grol thar te/ skye shi 'bab las 'das
90b8(mdo sde): te/ sems can dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal las phyin to// byang chub sems dpa' sems gcig gi chos 'di ming gcig ni 'gyod tshangs gyis grol thar pa zhes kyang bya ste/ yang dag
91a1(mdo sde): / pa'i bden pa'i gzhung mthong ba'i phyir ro// gnyisu na ming chos spyad pas grol thar ces kyang bya ste/ mnags gcig na 'dug pa'i phyir ro// gsum du na ming spyad pa med pas
91a2(mdo sde): grol thar ces kyang bya ste/ 'dug cing chags pa med pa'i phyiro// grol thar pa 'dris gsum ni kun kyang sems gcig las skyes te/ sems can thams cad la sems gnyis su med
91a3(mdo sde): ba'i phyir ro// sems can thams cad kun la theg pa gcig pu yod do// byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi rgyal po chos gcig kyang shes par nus na chos gcig mi shes pa med do// chos
91a4(mdo sde): gcig mi shes na chos gcig kyang shes pa med de// ci lta nas byas na chos rnams mi gcig pa med pa'i phyir ro// byang chub sems dpa' 'di gcig pu ces na da ni nyu
91a5(mdo sde): du thos pa yin no// chos mi shes pa med pa de'i ming ni ma 'du shes pa'o// ci'i phyir zhes byas na chos so chog gi ngo bo nyid gtsang ma gcig la 'dus pa'i phyir ro// gcig
91a6(mdo sde): pa 'di mthong ba'i phyir ro// gcig pu 'di mthong na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi lus mthong ngo // ci'i phyir zhes byas na sangs rgyas so chog gi lus ni gtsang ma gcig las byung ba'i
91a7(mdo sde): phyir ro// btsang ma gcig gis ni sangs rgyas gcig gi lus dang / sangs rgyas kyi sa gcig dang / byang chub kyi sdong ba gcig yin no// rigs kyi bu be cos 'di'i nang nas
91a8(mdo sde): mya ngan 'khrugs pa'i rnams bcad ba dang mtshungs/ rtsa ba 'ba' zhig bcad kyi yal ga dang / 'dab ma mi gcad// ci'i phyir zhes byas na/ dpar mi la la zhig lus la dug mang
91b1(mdo sde): 'og ste/ lus na tsha ba la mda' phyung na ni nad kyang sos so// mdar ma phyung na ni nang kyang mi ses so// de'i la bsdang de mnga' de'i sgron ci'i sgo/ gcig tu na de'i sdug rig las byung / 
91b2(mdo sde): mnga' de sus 'phang sa zhes 'dri na de'i bar du mi de/ na tsha bas tshe srog zad zin to// de'i 'og tu mnga' byung ba na phan pa med par mngon no// rigs kyi bu bo sems mang bzhin
91b3(mdo sde): khrus shig/ sems gtsang mar 'dug na de'i ming ni gtsang mnga' zhes bya'o// 'du mched kyi rnams gtsang gdang na yod pa la chags pa'i rnams dang bral te/ chags pa
91b4(mdo sde): meng pa'i nang du chud par nuso// ci'i phyir zhes byas na phyi mo sems can la bslabs te/ sman bzang po 'di bshad// nad kyi rnams gses la kun sos par 'tshal lo// yang
91b5(mdo sde): gcig tu na chos kyi yi ge 'dir rdo rje shes rab kyi gris sems can rnams kyi rig pa'i yid breg go// / yang gcig tu na chos kyi yi ge 'di gtsang gdang ba'i
91b6(mdo sde): chos spyad de// sems can rnams kyi gdugs pa gsum gyi dri ma brdab cing bas lo// yang gcig tu na chos kyi yi ge 'di shes rab kyi stobs po che/ spyad de sems can dkris

91b8(mdo sde): gcig/ sangs rgyas gcig/ ngo bo gcig/ gtsang gdang gcig/ thob ste/ theg pa tshigs kyi nang du chud yang dag par 'tshal lo// sems can rnams dmyal ba nas
92a1(mdo sde): // zar yang dag par 'tshal lo// sems can dmyal ba nas thar yang dag par 'tsha lo// bdag gis sems can gyi rnams bsngal ba'i ra mda' nus te/ sems can gyi rnams
92a2(mdo sde): sems can dmyal ba rnams lhung na/ bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi sku lus nub cing med par bgyis pa lags na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas kyi chos 'di bdag la gtad cing gangam
92a3(mdo sde): bar smon to// bdag la yang sems can rgya ces bsgrol ba bshad de/ sems can gyi rnams thos panyung la shes pa mang / mthong ba nyung la rig pa mang / yi ga'i ri me mang du ma 'tshal
92a4(mdo sde): bar gzhung gi mngon brtags thob ste/ chos nyung ngus/ yang dag bur grol thar la/ gzhan dog pa 'dri ba ma mchis par bgyi na/ sangs rgyas kyis byams shing thugs rje gzigs
92a5(mdo sde): / bdag la dgrol bshang par smon to// sangs rgyas kyis phal mang po la bka' stsal pa/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi rgyal po 'dis bskal pa brgya stong khri 'jam
92a6(mdo sde): gyi sangs rgyas rnams la yon gsol myong zin pas na/ thabs spyod pa mkhas te/ sems can rnams la ra mnga' bya zhing bsgral nuso// byang chub sems dpa' 'dis re dra ba'i

277b1(mdo sde): chos rnams spangs pas dge ba'i chos la zhugs pa yin no// skyes bungs bdag ni dngul po rnams kyi gter yin no// skyes grangs pa dpo mi nang pa rnams kyi sman pa yin no// skyes
277b2(mdo sde): dam pa dang ni 'jigs rten pa rnams kyi mngon yin no// skyes bu dam dag ni dadung gnyen med pa rnams kyi skyobs yin no// skyes bu dam pa dag ni 'khor ba'i rgya mtshar
277b3(mdo sde): zhugs pa rnams kyi banas yid ro// skyes bu dam pa dang ni rten meng pa rnams kyi can te// skyes bu dam pa dag ni mun pa mun nag tu zhugs pa rnams kyi snang bar byed pa yin// 
277b4(mdo sde): skyes bu ngam pa dang ni lam ngan par zhugs pa rnams kyi 'dren pa'i mo// skyes bu dag ni chos smrab rnams kyi yongs 'dren pa la no// skyes bu dam pa dag ni bzod pa dang dul ba'i
277b5(mdo sde): rnal 'byar dang ldan pas// tha ba'i nyes pa dang dan da sems dang // mnod 'chal pa dang // khro ba'i yongasu gdung ba thams cad dang bral ba yin te// de lhungs na skyes bu

277b7(mdo sde): byan pa sgom pa'i rnal 'byor dang ldan pas snying rje chen po la gnas pa rgyun mi chad pa// dpung po dang rtag tu dga' zhing 'god pa 'dod pi re dga' ba thams cad la btang snyom su ba

278a1(mdo sde): // mtshungs pa/ shes rab ma mkha' dang mtshungs pa/ shes rab namakha' rang mtshungs pas thams cad mkhyen pa rtogs par nuso// byang chub sems dpa' sems cu

278a3(mdo sde): lha mi dga' bar 'gyur ba dang / bdag gi dge ba'i ngogasu yongasu 'bri bar 'gyur ba'i sems bskyed pa de dag ni/ byang chub sems dngas me sbyad par bya'o// sems bskyed pa gang
278a4(mdo sde): las bdud sngog car gyis glags rung par mi 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / lha dag dga' bar 'gyur ba dang / bdag gi dag
278a5(mdo sde): byags yongasu 'bri bar mi 'gyur ba'i sems bskyed ba de dag ni bskyeng bar bya ste/ de da ltar zhugs na sems spyad ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor la sbyar bar
278a6(mdo sde): 'ogyuraro// ngo ci'i phyir zhe ma/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' des sems spyad ma thab tu rgyu dang ngarigs pa'i rkyen ma skye ba'i byed/ chos tham cad skyes pa dang / de bzhin pa

278b1(mdo sde): kyi rjesu song ba ste/ kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rje sung rnam par byang ba'i rjesu song ba/ 'dus byas kyi rjesu song ba/ 'dus ma pas kyi nasu song ba/ drag pa dang bcas pa'i

278b4(mdo sde): dang rtag pa'i rjesu song ba/ phung po dang khams dang / skye ma ched kyi rjesu song ba te/ skyes bu dam pa dag byang chub ni sa dang / chu dang / me dang rlung dang / namamakha'i

279a2(mdo sde): g.yo bar 'dug pa yin te/ sman par smras pa dang / mi snyan par smras pa la dga' ba dang / zhum pa mdo// 'di lta snga dbar ma'i ldan pa'i phung po la rlung rab pa lnga sngar

279a5(mdo sde): tshig kyang chos mnyam pa nyid du mthong mnyam pa nyid la'ang 'gal bar mi byeng / mu stegs can thams can gyi spongs pa thams cad kyang zad pa'i che su mthong zang

279a7(mdo sde): skye bar 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' blo gros rgya mtshos smras pa/ skyes rungs pa dag byang chub sems dpas thos pa thams cad gzung ba'i phyir/ blo rgya mtsho la sems 'jug pa
279a8(mdo sde): rtogs par byar// chos nyid la sna tshogs meng pa'i phyir des chos ro gcig pa la mos par bya'o// rten cing 'bral bar 'byung ba meng / mi dgal ba'i phyir// nges chos

279b4(mdo sde): 'chang ba'i phyir/ ngas skems pa thams cad yang dag por bcom pa yongasu rdzogs par bya'o// sangs rgyas kyi cho ma 'dres pa lhur byed pa'i phyir/ mi dge ba'i chos thams cad

279b7(mdo sde): rten thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa dang / thos pa 'jig rten thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa dang / dad pa 'jig rten thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa

280a1(mdo sde): rten thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa dang / bsod nams ri rab lhun po bzhin du mngon par 'phags pas thams cad mkhyen pa rtogs par nus/

280a3(mdo sde): snang ba yid du mi 'ong ba dang yang mig gis mthong zhing snang bar mi 'gyur// bdag gau sna ba'i sems yongasu dag pas sgra ying du mi 'ong ba gang yang rnabs thos shing

280b1(mdo sde): yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen du 'du shes skyed la bzod par byed/ bzod pa'i mthu ston cing rab tu dga' ba skyes nas/ skyo bar byed pa 'di su/ gang la spyo bar byed ces de ches cad kyi
280b2(mdo sde): rjesu 'jul par byed/ nang gi stong pa nyid la mos shing / bai'i stong pa nyid la the tshom med pas bdag tu lta ba'ang mo skyed cing bzong la/ rkang pa dang / lag pa yongasu gtong ba dang / mig

281a1(mdo sde): // shes med kyi/ rnam par rtog pa spyod pa ldang ma yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad mthong mod kyi bzugs la dmigs pa'i 'du shes kyang mi skyed// sems can thams
